0                                   1007              * LAST UPDATE 7/89
                                    1008              *******************************************************************
                                    1009              **                                                             ****
                                    1010              **                                                              ***
                                    1011              **      HOW TO ADD A SYSTEM VARIABLE OR FUNCTION !               **
                                    1012              ***     ------------------------------------------               **
                                    1013              *****                                                            **
                                    1014              *      FOR MORE INFORMATION SEE COMMENTS IN FUNC MODULE.          *
                                    1015              *******************************************************************
                                    1016              *
                                    1017              *  PROCEDURE TO ADD VARIABLE OR FUNCTION:
                                    1018              *
                                    1019              *  1. ADD A ENTRY INTO THE SYSTEM VARIABLE/FUNCTION TABLE.
                                    1020              *
                                    1021              *       THIS TABLE (SYSFNS) IS SEARCHED TO FIND THE ADDRESS OF
                                    1022              *       THE ROUTINE FOR THE SPECIFIED FUNCTION, VARIABLE, OR
                                    1023              *       PROC.  THE ENTRIES MUST APPEAR IN ALPHABETICAL ORDER.
                                    1024              *       USE THE 'SYSFN'    AND  'SYSVAR'   MACRO TO CREATE A
                                    1025              *       PROPERLY FORMATTED ENTRY.
                                    1026              *
                                    1027              *  2. ADD A SYSTEM VARIABLE/FUNCTION ROUTINE.
                                    1028              *
                                    1029              *       SYSTEM VARIABLE/FUNCTION ROUTINES ARE FOUND AFTER THE
                                    1030              *       SYSTEM VARIABLE/FUNCTION TABLE. THE ROUTINES SHOULD BE
                                    1031              *       PLACED IN ALPHABETICAL ORDER BASED ON THE VAR/FUNC
                                    1032              *       KEYWORD.  WORK AND COMMON ROUTINES SHOULD BE PLACED
                                    1033              *       IN ALPHABETICAL ORDER IN THE COMMON/WORK ROUTINES AREA.
                                    1034              *       THE BASIC ENTRY AND EXIT CONVENTIONS ARE:
                                    1035              *
                                    1036              *       ON ENTRY:
                                    1037              *            R0 - VARIABLE COUNT
                                    1038              *            R1 - ARGUMENT LIST    (FOR FUNCTIONS/PROC, ONLY)
                                    1039              *            R6 - FUNCTION/VARIABLE RETURN AREA
                                    1040              *                 (AREA WILL INITIALLY CONTAIN VAR/FUNC/PROC NAME)
                                    1041              *
                                    1042              *       ON EXIT:
                                    1043              *            R6 - RETURNED VALUE (SAME AS ON ENTRY)
                                    1044              *           R15 - CC=ZERO, ALL OK
                                    1045              *                 CC=NZ, IF ERROR,,, ERROR MSG TSEG 'D
                                    1046              *
                                    1047              *       THE FORMAT OF THE ARGUMENTS PASSED AND RETURNED IS
                                    1048              *       DESCRIBED BY THE VNENTRY DSECT.  EACH ARGUMENT OCCUPIES
                                    1049              *       A FIXED LENGTH (L'VPARM) ENTRY. THUS EACH INPUT
                                    1050              *       ARGUMENT (IF ANY) CAN BE EASILY FOUND AT A FIXED OFFSET
                                    1051              *       BASED OFF OF R1.
                                    1052              *
                                    1053              *       SEVERAL MACROS EXIST TO MAKE THE ADDITION OF ROUTINES
                                    1054              *       EASIER.  TO USE THESE MACROS CERTAIN ADDITIONAL
                                    1055              *       CONVENTIONS MUST BE ADHERED TO.  THESE CONVENTIONS AND
                                    1056              *       THE MACROS ARE DESCRIBED NOW:
                                    1057              *
                                    1058              *   *** AN 'PROC' AND AN 'PEND' MUST
                                    1059              *       BE USED TO ENTER AND EXIT THE ROUTINE.
                                    1060              *
                                    1061              *   *** IF THE ROUTINE IS SUCCESSFUL R15 MUST BE RETURNED
                                    1062              *       EQUAL TO ZERO.  IF NOT R15 MUST BE RETURNED AS NON-ZERO
1SYSV     WYLBUR System Variables                                                                                           Page    5
0D-Loc  Object Code    Addr1 Addr2  Stmt Lv Lineno    Source Statement           (Hibal 5, Asmedit 3.3)  HLASM R4.0  2004/03/15 12.56
+_____  ______ ____    _____ _____  ____ __ ______    ______ _________
0                                   1063              *       (4).  ALSO AN APPROPRIATE ERROR MESSAGE MUST BE TSEG'D.
                                    1064              *       ** DO NOT EXIT A ROUTINE VIA CVNEXT OR CVERROR !! **
                                    1065              *
                                    1066              *   *** IF YOU INTEND TO USE THE "SCANNER", YOU MUST SAVE AND
                                    1067              *       RESTORE THE CURRENT SCANNER STATE.  FOR AN EXAMPLE SEE
                                    1068              *       'YESNO' ROUTINE.
                                    1069              *
                                    1070              *   *** THE 'VRETURN' MACRO
                                    1071              *
                                    1072              *       THE 'VRETURN' MACRO IS USED TO RETURN A VARIABLE OR
                                    1073              *       FUNCTION VALUE.  IT TAKES 2-3 PARAMETERS. THE FIRST IS
                                    1074              *       THE TYPE OF VALUE TO RETURN.  THIS MAY BE STRING,
                                    1075              *       INTEGER, LINENO, OR BOOLEAN.  ARRAYS AND PACKED NUMBERS
                                    1076              *       MAY NOT BE RETURNED WITH THIS MACRO.  ARGUMENTS 2-3 ARE
                                    1077              *       THE VALUE OF THE VAR/FUNC.  IF THE TYPE IS A STRING:
                                    1078              *       ARGS 2-3 ARE THE STRING LOC, LENGTH; A QUOTED STRING
                                    1079              *       MAY BE RETURNED, THE CONVENTIONS FOR RETURNING A STRING
                                    1080              *       ARE THE SAME AS FOR THE 'MSG' MACRO.  IF THE TYPE IS
                                    1081              *       INTEGER OR LINENO: THE SECOND PARAMETER IS A FULLWORD
                                    1082              *       VALUE.  IF THE TYPE IS BOOLEAN: THE SECOND PARAMETER IS
                                    1083              *       THE WORD 'TRUE' OR THE WORD 'FALSE'.  THIS MACRO
                                    1084              *       REQUIRES THAT R6 BE THE SAME AS WHEN THE SYSTEM
                                    1085              *       VAR/FUNC. ROUTINE WAS ENTERED.  FOR EXAMPLES, SEE THE
                                    1086              *       'FNCASE' 'FNLENGTH' 'FNLILB' 'FNLAST' AND 'FNTRUE'.
                                    1087              *       SOME ISOLATED EXAMPLES ARE:
                                    1088              *             VRETURN STRING,' THIS IS IT '
                                    1089              *             VRETURN STRING,(R1),(R0)
                                    1090              *             VRETURN BOOLEAN,TRUE
                                    1091              *             VRETURN LINENO,L:XXLINENO
                                    1092              *             VRETURN INTEGER,(R4)
                                    1093              *       HEY DUDE !! THE VRETURN MACRO CLOBBERS R15,R0,R1,R2 SO
                                    1094              *       BE CAREFUL.  R15 IS SET TO ZERO BY THE VRETURN MACRO.
                                    1095              *
                                    1096              *   *** THE 'VTRIM' MACRO
                                    1097              *
                                    1098              *       THE 'VTRIM' MACRO IS USED TO TRIM TRAILING BLANKS OFF
                                    1099              *       THE END OF RETURNED STINGS.  IT WILL ALSO SET BLANK OR
                                    1100              *       ZEROED STRINGS TO NULL STRINGS.  IT REQUIRES THAT R6 BE
                                    1101              *       THE SAVE AS WHEN THE SYSTEM FUNC/VAR ROUTINE WAS
                                    1102              *       ENTERED.  IT IS GENERALLY CODED DIRECTLY FOLLOWING THE
                                    1103              *       'VRETURN STRING,..' MACRO.  FOR AN EXAMPLE SEE 'FNLIB'
                                    1104              *       ROUTINE.
                                    1105              *
                                    1106              *
                                    1107              *
                                    1108              *   *** RETURNING VAR/FUNCTION VALUE,,,
                                    1109              *
                                    1110              *       THE EASY WAY IS WITH THE 'VRETURN MACRO', BUT THERE ARE
                                    1111              *       OTHER WAYS.  YOU MAY SET UP YOUR OWN RETURN VALUE @R6.
                                    1112              *       SEE VNENTRY DSECT. THE AREA MUST BE CLEARED.  FLAGS
                                    1113              *       MUST BE SET FOR THE VARIABLE TYPE:  STRING, BOOLEAN,
                                    1114              *       NUMBER.  THE VARIABLE VALUE MUST BE SET.  FOR EXAMPLES,
                                    1115              *       SEE 'FNASCII' 'FNPI' OR 'FNSUBSTR'.  IF YOU WANT TO
                                    1116              *       DEAL WITH ARRAYS (IF THEY EXIST),,, GOOD LUCK HASBRO !!
                                    1117              *
                                    1118              *   *** FINAL ADVICE

                                    1120              *       THIS MODULE ADHERES TO SEVERAL CONVENTIONS.  IF YOU
                                    1121              *       ADHERE TO THESE CONVENTIONS, IT WILL MAKE IT EASIER FOR
                                    1122              *       YOU AND ALL THE PEOPLE WHO ALSO WANT TO ADD VARS/FUNCS
                                    1123              *       TO ADD THEM. IT IS WORTH IT TO TAKE A BIT OF TIME AND
                                    1124              *       LOOK AT HOW SEVERAL EXITING SYSTEM VARIABLE/FUNCTION

                                    1126              *

                                    1129              *        ON ENTRY:
